Source Code

These source-code files were transcribed from a printout in Don Eyles's personal collection, scanned by archive.org, and financially sponsored by Linden Sims. A team of volunteers performed the transcription and proof-reading. The scanned page images are available at the Virtual AGC Project website, as well as higher-quality (but much larger) images at the Virtual AGC Project's collection in the Internet Archive. Report any problems by creating "issues" at the Virtual AGC Project's GitHub Repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 56 OF AGC PROGRAM ZERLINA BY ZOROASTER
	9:12 OCT. 21,1970
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

022373,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
022374,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
022375,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A log section of Zerlina 56, the final revision of
022376,000005:                                                                                                  ##              Don Eyles's offline development program for the variable 
022377,000006:                                                                                                  ##              guidance period servicer. It also includes a new P66 with LPD 
022378,000007:                                                                                                  ##              (Landing Point Designator) capability, based on an idea of John 
022379,000008:                                                                                                  ##              Young's. Neither of these advanced features were actually flown,
022380,000009:                                                                                                  ##              but Zerlina was also the birthplace of other big improvements to
022381,000010:                                                                                                  ##              Luminary including the terrain model and new (Luminary 1E)
022382,000011:                                                                                                  ##              analog display programs. Zerlina was branched off of Luminary 145,
022383,000012:                                                                                                  ##              and revision 56 includes all changes up to and including Luminary
022384,000013:                                                                                                  ##              183. It is therefore quite close to the Apollo 14 program,
022385,000014:                                                                                                  ##              Luminary 178, where not modified with new features.
022386,000015:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 500-611
022387,000016:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
022388,000017:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
022389,000018:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
022390,000019:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2017-07-28 MAS  Created from Luminary 210.
022391,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2017-08-20 MAS  Began updates for Zerlina 56.
022392,000021:                                                                                                  ##              2017-08-22 MAS  Completed updating for Zerlina.
022393,000022:

Page 500 

022395,000024:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
022396,000025:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022397,000026:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022398,000027:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022399,000028:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022400,000029: 
022401,000030:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
022402,000031:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
022403,000032:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
022404,000033:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
022405,000034:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022406,000035: 
022407,000036:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
022408,000037:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022409,000038:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
022410,000039:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
022411,000040:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
022412,000041:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
022413,000042:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
022414,000043:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
022415,000044:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
022416,000045:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
022417,000046:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)    
022418,000047:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
022419,000048:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022420,000049:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022421,000050:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022422,000051:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022423,000052:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
022424,000053:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022425,000054:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
022426,000055:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022427,000056:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022428,000057:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
022429,000058:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022430,000059:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
022431,000060: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
022432,000061: 
022433,000062: 33,2031                                           BANK     33                                    
022434,000063: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
022435,000064: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
022436,000065: 
022437,000066: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022438,000067: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
022439,000068: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
022440,000069: 24,2000           05340        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022441,000070: 24,2001           00004                           OCT      4                                     
022442,000071: 24,2002           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022443,000072: 24,2003           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022444,000073: 24,2004           02752                           TC       LUNSFCHK                              #  CHECK IF ON LUNAR SURFACE

022920,000549:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022921,000550:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022922,000551:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022923,000552:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022924,000553:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022925,000554: 
022926,000555:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022927,000556:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022928,000557:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022929,000558:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022930,000559:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022931,000560:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022932,000561:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022933,000562:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022934,000563:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022935,000564:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022936,000565:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022937,000566:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022938,000567:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022939,000568:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022940,000569:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022941,000570:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022942,000571:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022943,000572:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022944,000573:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022945,000574:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022946,000575:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022947,000576:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022948,000577: 24,2462  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022949,000578: 24,2462                                           COUNT*   $$/P25                                
022950,000579: 24,2462           05340        PROG25             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022951,000580: 24,2463           00004                           OCT      4                                     #  MAKE GROUP 4 INACTIVE (VERB 37)
022952,000581: 24,2464           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022953,000582: 24,2465           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022954,000583: 
022955,000584: 24,2466           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022956,000585: 24,2467           11241                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
022957,000586: 24,2470           05515                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022958,000587: 24,2471           00031                           ADRES    TRACKFLG                              #  SET TRACK FLAG
022959,000588: 24,2472           05515                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022960,000589: 24,2473           00006                           ADRES    P25FLAG                               #  SET P25FLAG
022961,000590: 24,2474           05527                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              
022962,000591: 24,2475           00010                           ADRES    RNDVZFLG

022966,000595: 24,2501           70074                           MASK     STATE                                 #  IS P25FLAG SET
022967,000596: 24,2502           00006                           EXTEND

Page 512 

022971,000600: 24,2505           70075                           MASK     STATE      +1                         
022972,000601: 24,2506           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022973,000602: 24,2507           12515                           BZF      P25LMWT1                              #  NO-SKIP PHASE CHANGE AND WAIT 1 MINUTE
022974,000603: 24,2510           34757                           CAF      SEVEN                                 #  CALL R65 - FINE PREFERRED
022975,000604: 24,2511           55745                           TS       R65CNTR

022992,000621:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022993,000622:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022994,000623:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022995,000624:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022996,000625:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022997,000626: 
022998,000627:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022999,000628:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
023000,000629:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023001,000630:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023002,000631:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM

023004,000633:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
023005,000634:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
023006,000635:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
023007,000636:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023008,000637:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
023009,000638:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
023010,000639:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.

023013,000642:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
023014,000643:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT

023196,000825:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
023197,000826:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023198,000827:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023199,000828:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023200,000829:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023201,000830: 
023202,000831:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
023203,000832:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
023204,000833:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023205,000834:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023206,000835:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM

023208,000837:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
023209,000838:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG

023211,000840:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
023212,000841:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
023213,000842:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
023214,000843:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
023215,000844:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023216,000845:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
023217,000846:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
023218,000847:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
023219,000848:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT

023222,000851:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM

023402,001031:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
023403,001032:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023404,001033:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023405,001034:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023406,001035:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023407,001036: 
023408,001037:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023409,001038:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023410,001039:                                                                                                  #           TC     R23LEM
023411,001040:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023412,001041:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL        R61LEM
023413,001042:                                                                                                  #    SETMINDB        GOPERF1
023414,001043:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
023415,001044:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
023416,001045:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF PROC  WILL CONTINUE R23
023417,001046:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF TERM  WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
023418,001047:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
023419,001048:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023420,001049:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023421,001050:                                                                                                  #    N.A.
023422,001051:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED-
023423,001052:                                                                                                  #    ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
023424,001053: 24,3221     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
023425,001054: 24,3221                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
023426,001055: 24,3221           05515        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
023427,001056: 24,3222           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
023428,001057: 24,3223           00004                           INHINT                                         
023429,001058: 24,3224           04674                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
023430,001059: 24,3225           40141                           CADR     SETMINDB

023472,001101:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
023473,001102:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023474,001103:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023475,001104:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
023476,001105:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023477,001106: 
023478,001107:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
023479,001108:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
023480,001109:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
023481,001110:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
023482,001111:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
023483,001112:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
023484,001113:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
023485,001114:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
023486,001115:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023487,001116:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
023488,001117:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
023489,001118:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
023490,001119:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023491,001120:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
023492,001121:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
023493,001122:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
023494,001123:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023495,001124:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023496,001125:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
023497,001126:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
023498,001127:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023499,001128:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
023500,001129:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023501,001130:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
023502,001131: 24,3272  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
023503,001132: 24,3272                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
023504,001133: 24,3272           05515        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
023505,001134: 24,3273           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
023506,001135: 24,3274           05527                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
023507,001136: 24,3275           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
023508,001137: 24,3276           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
023509,001138: 24,3277           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR

023511,001140: 24,3301           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS

023573,001202:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
023574,001203:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023575,001204:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO : 3                      DATE : 4-11-67
023576,001205:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY : P VOLANTE  SDC
023577,001206: 
023578,001207: 
023579,001208:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
023580,001209:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
023581,001210:                                                                                                  #  TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED

023784,001413:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023785,001414: 
023786,001415:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023787,001416:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023788,001417:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023789,001418:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023790,001419:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023791,001420:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023792,001421:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023793,001422:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023794,001423:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023795,001424:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023796,001425:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023797,001426:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023798,001427:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023799,001428:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023800,001429:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023801,001430: 
023802,001431:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023803,001432:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
023804,001433:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES T,S   (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
023805,001434: 
023806,001435:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023807,001436:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
023808,001437:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023809,001438:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
023810,001439: 
023811,001440:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
023812,001441: 
023813,001442:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023814,001443: 
023815,001444:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023816,001445: 
023817,001446:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L + 2 (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023818,001447:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023819,001448: 
023820,001449:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

023863,001492:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023864,001493: 
023865,001494:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023866,001495:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023867,001496:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023868,001497:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023869,001498:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023870,001499:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023871,001500:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023872,001501:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023873,001502:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023874,001503:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023875,001504:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023876,001505:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023877,001506:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023878,001507:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023879,001508:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023880,001509:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023881,001510:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023882,001511:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023883,001512:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023884,001513:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023885,001514: 
023886,001515:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023887,001516:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  SETTRKF
023888,001517: 
023889,001518:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
023890,001519:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
023891,001520: 
023892,001521:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023893,001522: 
023894,001523:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP

023933,001562:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
023934,001563: 
023935,001564:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023936,001565: 
023937,001566:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
023938,001567:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023939,001568:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023940,001569:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023941,001570:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023942,001571:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023943,001572:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023944,001573:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023945,001574:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023946,001575:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023947,001576:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023948,001577:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023949,001578: 
023950,001579:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023951,001580:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
023952,001581:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023953,001582: 
023954,001583:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023955,001584:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023956,001585: 
023957,001586:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023958,001587: 
023959,001588:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023960,001589:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023961,001590: 
023962,001591:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023963,001592: 
023964,001593:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023965,001594: 
023966,001595: 24,3340                                           BANK     24                                    
023967,001596: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023968,001597: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023969,001598: 
023970,001599: 25,2053  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023971,001600: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023972,001601: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
023973,001602: 25,2054           05232                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
023974,001603: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.
023975,001604: 25,2056           44753                           CS       TURNONBT

023981,001610:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023982,001611: 
023983,001612:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023984,001613:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023985,001614:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023986,001615:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023987,001616:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023988,001617:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
023989,001618:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023990,001619:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023991,001620:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023992,001621:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023993,001622:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023994,001623:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023995,001624:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023996,001625:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023997,001626:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023998,001627:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023999,001628: 
024000,001629:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
024001,001630:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024002,001631:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
024003,001632: 
024004,001633:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
024005,001634: 
024006,001635:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024007,001636:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024008,001637: 
024009,001638:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
024010,001639: 
024011,001640:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
024012,001641: 
024013,001642: 25,2062           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
024014,001643: 25,2063           23312                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
024015,001644: 25,2064           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
024016,001645: 25,2065           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
024017,001646: 25,2066           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
024018,001647: 25,2067           05232                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
024019,001648: 25,2070           00002                           DEC      2          B-14

024054,001683:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
024055,001684:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024056,001685:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
024057,001686:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
024058,001687:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
024059,001688:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
024060,001689:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
024061,001690:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
024062,001691:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
024063,001692:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
024064,001693:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
024065,001694:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
024066,001695:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
024067,001696:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
024068,001697:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
024069,001698:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
024070,001699:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
024071,001700:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
024072,001701:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
024073,001702:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024074,001703:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
024075,001704:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
024076,001705:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
024077,001706:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
024078,001707: 
024079,001708:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024080,001709:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
024081,001710:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
024082,001711: 
024083,001712:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024084,001713:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
024085,001714: 
024086,001715:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024087,001716:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
024088,001717: 
024089,001718:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024090,001719:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024091,001720: 
024092,001721:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
024093,001722: 
024094,001723:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
024095,001724:

024141,001770:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
024142,001771: 
024143,001772:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
024144,001773:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
024145,001774:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
024146,001775:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
024147,001776:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
024148,001777:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
024149,001778:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
024150,001779:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
024151,001780:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
024152,001781:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
024153,001782:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
024154,001783:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
024155,001784:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
024156,001785:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
024157,001786:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
024158,001787:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
024159,001788:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
024160,001789:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
024161,001790:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
024162,001791:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
024163,001792: 
024164,001793:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024165,001794:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
024166,001795:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
024167,001796:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
024168,001797:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
024169,001798: 
024170,001799:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024171,001800:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
024172,001801: 
024173,001802:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024174,001803:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
024175,001804: 
024176,001805:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024177,001806:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024178,001807: 
024179,001808:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024180,001809: 
024181,001810:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  STDESIG
024182,001811:

024234,001863:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
024235,001864: 
024236,001865:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024237,001866:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
024238,001867:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
024239,001868:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
024240,001869:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
024241,001870:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
024242,001871:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
024243,001872:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
024244,001873:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
024245,001874:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
024246,001875:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
024247,001876:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
024248,001877:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
024249,001878:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
024250,001879:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
024251,001880: 
024252,001881:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE*  (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
024253,001882:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
024254,001883:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
024255,001884:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
024256,001885:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
024257,001886: 
024258,001887:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024259,001888:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
024260,001889:

024265,001894:                                                                                                  #  NONE

024322,001951:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
024323,001952: 
024324,001953:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024325,001954:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
024326,001955:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
024327,001956:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
024328,001957:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
024329,001958:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
024330,001959:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
024331,001960:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
024332,001961:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
024333,001962:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
024334,001963:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
024335,001964:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
024336,001965:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
024337,001966:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024338,001967: 
024339,001968:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024340,001969:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
024341,001970:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
024342,001971: 
024343,001972:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024344,001973:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
024345,001974:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).

024428,002057:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
024429,002058: 
024430,002059:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024431,002060:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
024432,002061:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
024433,002062:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
024434,002063:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
024435,002064:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
024436,002065:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
024437,002066:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
024438,002067:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
024439,002068:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
024440,002069:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
024441,002070:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
024442,002071:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
024443,002072:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
024444,002073:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
024445,002074:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
024446,002075:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
024447,002076:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
024448,002077:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
024449,002078:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
024450,002079:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
024451,002080:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
024452,002081:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
024453,002082: 
024454,002083:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024455,002084:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
024456,002085:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
024457,002086:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024458,002087:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024459,002088: 
024460,002089:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024461,002090:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
024462,002091: 
024463,002092:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024464,002093:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
024465,002094:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
024466,002095: 
024467,002096:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024468,002097:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024469,002098: 
024470,002099:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024471,002100: 
024472,002101:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
024473,002102:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
024474,002103:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
