024514,002143:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
024515,002144: 
024516,002145:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
024517,002146:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
024518,002147:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024519,002148:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
024520,002149:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
024521,002150:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024522,002151:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
024523,002152:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
024524,002153:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
024525,002154:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
024526,002155:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
024527,002156:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
024528,002157:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
024529,002158:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
024530,002159:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
024531,002160:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
024532,002161:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
024533,002162:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
024534,002163:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
024535,002164:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
024536,002165:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024537,002166: 
024538,002167:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024539,002168:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
024540,002169:

024542,002171:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)

024686,002315:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024687,002316: 
024688,002317:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024689,002318:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024690,002319:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024691,002320:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024692,002321:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024693,002322:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024694,002323:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024695,002324:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024696,002325:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024697,002326:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024698,002327:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024699,002328:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024700,002329:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024701,002330:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024702,002331:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024703,002332:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024704,002333:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024705,002334:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024706,002335:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024707,002336:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024708,002337:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024709,002338:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024710,002339:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024711,002340:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024712,002341:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024713,002342:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024714,002343: 
024715,002344:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024716,002345:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024717,002346:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024718,002347:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024719,002348: 
024720,002349:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024721,002350:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024722,002351: 
024723,002352:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024724,002353:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024725,002354: 
024726,002355:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024727,002356: 
024728,002357:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024729,002358:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024730,002359: 
024731,002360:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024732,002361:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024733,002362:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024734,002363: 
024735,002364: 25,2564           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

024781,002410:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024782,002411: 
024783,002412:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024784,002413:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024785,002414:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024786,002415:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024787,002416:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024788,002417:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024789,002418:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024790,002419:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024791,002420:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024792,002421:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
024793,002422:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024794,002423:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024795,002424:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
024796,002425:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024797,002426:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024798,002427:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024799,002428:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024800,002429:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024801,002430:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024802,002431:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024803,002432:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024804,002433:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024805,002434:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024806,002435:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024807,002436:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024808,002437:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024809,002438:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024810,002439:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024811,002440:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024812,002441:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024813,002442:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024814,002443:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024815,002444:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024816,002445:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024817,002446:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024818,002447:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024819,002448:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024820,002449:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024821,002450: 
024822,002451:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024823,002452:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024824,002453: 
024825,002454:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024826,002455:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024827,002456:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024828,002457: 
024829,002458:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024830,002459:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
024831,002460:

Page 557 

024833,002462:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024834,002463:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024835,002464: 
024836,002465:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024837,002466: 
024838,002467:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)

025767,003396:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025768,003397:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025769,003398: 
025770,003399: 
025771,003400:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025772,003401: 
025773,003402:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025774,003403:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025775,003404:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025776,003405: 
025777,003406:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025778,003407: 
025779,003408: 
025780,003409:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025781,003410: 
025782,003411: 
025783,003412:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025784,003413: 
025785,003414:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
025786,003415:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025787,003416:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025788,003417:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025789,003418:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025790,003419: 
025791,003420: 
025792,003421:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025793,003422: 
025794,003423:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025795,003424:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025796,003425: 
025797,003426: 
025798,003427:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025799,003428:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025800,003429: 
025801,003430: 
025802,003431:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025803,003432:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025804,003433: 
025805,003434:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025806,003435: 
025807,003436:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025808,003437:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025809,003438:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025810,003439:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
025811,003440:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
025812,003441: 
025813,003442: 
025814,003443:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025815,003444: 
025816,003445:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 582 

025818,003447:                                                                                                  #      1)RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
025819,003448:                                                                                                  #      2)RR RANGE RATE,SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT

026021,003650:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
026022,003651:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
026023,003652:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
026024,003653: 
026025,003654:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026026,003655: 
026027,003656:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
026028,003657:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
026029,003658:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
026030,003659: 
026031,003660:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
026032,003661:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
026033,003662:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
026034,003663:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
026035,003664:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
026036,003665:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
026037,003666:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
026038,003667: 
026039,003668: 
026040,003669:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026041,003670:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
026042,003671:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
026043,003672: 
026044,003673:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026045,003674:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026046,003675:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026047,003676:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026048,003677:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026049,003678:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026050,003679: 
026051,003680: 
026052,003681:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026053,003682:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
026054,003683:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
026055,003684:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
026056,003685:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
026057,003686:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
026058,003687:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
026059,003688:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
026060,003689:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
026061,003690:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
026062,003691:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
026063,003692:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
026064,003693:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
026065,003694:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
026066,003695:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
026067,003696: 
026068,003697:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026069,003698:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
026070,003699:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

026461,004090: 26,3201           50644                                    R22LEM93                              
026462,004091:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026463,004092: 
026464,004093:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
026465,004094:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
026466,004095:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
026467,004096: 
026468,004097:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026469,004098:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
026470,004099:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
026471,004100: 
026472,004101:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026473,004102:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026474,004103:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026475,004104:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026476,004105:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026477,004106:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026478,004107:

Page 596 

026480,004109:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026481,004110:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
026482,004111:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
026483,004112:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
026484,004113:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
026485,004114:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
026486,004115:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
026487,004116: 
026488,004117: 
026489,004118: 26,3202           77624        LSR22.4            CALL                                           
026490,004119: 26,3203           27410                                    INTSTALL                              
026491,004120: 26,3204           43014                           SET      CLEAR                                 
026492,004121: 26,3205           01472                                    STATEFLG                              
026493,004122: 26,3206           01674                                    VINTFLAG                              #  CALL TO GET LM POS + VEL IN REF COORD.
026494,004123: 26,3207           77624                           CALL                                           
026495,004124: 26,3210           55244                                    INTGRCAL                              
026496,004125: 26,3211           77624                           CALL                                           
026497,004126: 26,3212           11216                                    GRP2PC

026685,004314:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
026686,004315:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
026687,004316: 
026688,004317: 
026689,004318:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026690,004319: 
026691,004320:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
026692,004321:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
026693,004322:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
026694,004323:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
026695,004324: 
026696,004325: 
026697,004326:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026698,004327: 
026699,004328: 
026700,004329:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026701,004330: 
026702,004331:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026703,004332:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026704,004333:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026705,004334:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026706,004335:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026707,004336: 
026708,004337: 
026709,004338:                                                                                                  #  EXIT  - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026710,004339: 
026711,004340: 
026712,004341:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026713,004342: 
026714,004343:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026715,004344:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026716,004345:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026717,004346: 
026718,004347:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026719,004348:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026720,004349:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026721,004350:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026722,004351: 
026723,004352:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026724,004353:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026725,004354:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026726,004355:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026727,004356:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026728,004357: 
026729,004358: 
026730,004359: 26,3444                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
026731,004360: 26,3444           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
026732,004361: 26,3445           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
026733,004362: 26,3446           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
026734,004363: 26,3447           00006                           EXTEND
